namespace = lia_event_rlg

####1~99까지는 도시별 저널관련 이벤트 외 이벤들 전용 슬롯

lia_event_rlg.1 = { #서울
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT

	title = lia_event_rlg.1.t
	desc = lia_event_rlg.1.d
	flavor = lia_event_rlg.1.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/juncha.png"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/africa/city_center"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.1.a
		default_option = yes
		s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL = {
			create_state = {
				country = c:KOR
				owned_provinces = { 
					"xA0E2EE"
				}
			}
			add_homeland = korean
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_rlg_seoul_1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
            s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL = {
                region_state:KOR = {
                    create_building = {
                        building = "building_construction_sector"
                        level = 5
                    }
                    create_building = {
                        building = "building_government_administration"
                        level = 5
                    }
                    create_building = {
                        building = "building_university"
                        level = 5
                    }
                    create_building = {
                        building = "building_trade_center"
                        level = 1
                    }
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_newcity
                        months = 12
                        #is_decaying = yes
                    }
                }
            }
            s:STATE_SEOUL = {
                region_state:KOR = {
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = korean
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:sephardic
                            value = 0.10
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            s:STATE_SEOUL = {
                region_state:KOR = {
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = sephardic
                        }
                        move_pop = s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR
                    }
                }
            }
            s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = sephardic
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:korean
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                add_modifier = {
                    name = lia_rlg_modi_seoul_metro_1
                }
            }
            set_capital = STATE_LIA_SEOUL
            if = {
                limit = {
                    NOT = { has_variable = lia_var_rlg_add_2 }
                    NOT = { has_variable = lia_var_rlg_add_3 }
                }
                every_scope_state = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_KAESONG
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_NAMPHO
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_UIJU
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_WONSAN
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_ULSAN
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_DAEGU
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_DAEJEON
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_GWANGJU
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_JEJU
                        }
                    }
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_1
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_2
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_3
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_1
                    }
                }
                every_scope_state = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            state_region = s:STATE_SEOUL
                            state_region = s:STATE_PYONGYANG
                            state_region = s:STATE_SARIWON
                            state_region = s:STATE_BUSAN
                            state_region = s:STATE_YANGHO
                        }
                    }
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_1
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_2
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_3
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_1
                    }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    has_variable = lia_var_rlg_add_2
                    NOT = { has_variable = lia_var_rlg_add_3 }
                }
                every_scope_state = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_KAESONG
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_NAMPHO
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_UIJU
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_WONSAN
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_ULSAN
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_DAEGU
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_DAEJEON
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_GWANGJU
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_JEJU
                        }
                    }
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_1
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_2
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_3
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_2
                    }
                }
                every_scope_state = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            state_region = s:STATE_SEOUL
                            state_region = s:STATE_PYONGYANG
                            state_region = s:STATE_SARIWON
                            state_region = s:STATE_BUSAN
                            state_region = s:STATE_YANGHO
                        }
                    }
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_1
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_2
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_3
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_2
                    }
                }
            }
            else = {
                every_scope_state = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_KAESONG
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_NAMPHO
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_UIJU
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_WONSAN
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_ULSAN
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_DAEGU
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_DAEJEON
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_GWANGJU
                            state_region = s:STATE_LIA_JEJU
                        }
                    }
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_1
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_2
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_3
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_3
                    }
                }
                every_scope_state = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            state_region = s:STATE_SEOUL
                            state_region = s:STATE_PYONGYANG
                            state_region = s:STATE_SARIWON
                            state_region = s:STATE_BUSAN
                            state_region = s:STATE_YANGHO
                        }
                    }
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_1
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_2
                    remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_3
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_3
                    }
                }
            }
		}
	}
}

lia_event_rlg.5 = { #국고보조금 투입
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT

	title = lia_event_rlg.5.t
	desc = lia_event_rlg.5.desc
	flavor = lia_event_rlg.5.flavor

	duration = 1
    is_popup = yes

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/rlg/rlg_koreamap1900.png"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/africa/city_center"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { has_global_variable = lia_rlg_glovar_imsibosang }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_bosang
            set_global_variable = lia_rlg_glovar_imsibosang
        }
	}

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.5.a
        
        trigger = {
            NOT = { has_law = law_type:law_closed_borders }
        }
        
        trigger_event = {
            id = lia_event_rlg.30
        }
	}
	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.5.b
        
        trigger = {
            NOT = { has_law = law_type:law_serfdom }
            any_scope_state = {
				state_region = { 
                    is_homeland = cu:korean
				}
            }
        }
        
        trigger_event = {
            id = lia_event_rlg.31
        }
	}
	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.5.c
        
        trigger = {
            NOT = { has_law = law_type:law_serfdom }
            any_scope_state = {
				state_region = { 
                    is_homeland = cu:japanese
				}
            }
        }
        
        trigger_event = {
            id = lia_event_rlg.32
        }
	}
	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.5.d
        
        trigger = {
            NOT = { has_law = law_type:law_serfdom }
            any_scope_state = {
				state_region = { 
                    OR = {
                        is_homeland = cu:han
                        is_homeland = cu:manchu
                    }
				}
            }
        }
        
        trigger_event = {
            id = lia_event_rlg.33
        }
	}
	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.5.e
        
        trigger = {
            OR = {
                has_law = law_type:law_dedicated_police
                has_law = law_type:law_militarized_police
            }
        }
        
        trigger_event = {
            id = lia_event_rlg.34
        }
	}
	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.5.f
        
        trigger = {
            OR = {
                has_law = law_type:law_women_in_the_workplace
                has_law = law_type:law_womens_suffrage
            }
        }
        
        trigger_event = {
            id = lia_event_rlg.35
        }
	}
	#option = {
	#	name = lia_event_rlg.5.g
    #
	#}
	#option = {
	#	name = lia_event_rlg.5.h
    #
	#}
	#option = {
	#	name = lia_event_rlg.5.i
    #
	#}
    
	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.5.z
        remove_variable = lia_var_rlg_support
        
        default_option = yes
	}
}

##10~20번대는 새로승격할 도시유형 선택 이벤트 전용 슬롯
lia_event_rlg.10 = { #유형선택
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT

	title = lia_event_rlg.10.t
	desc = lia_event_rlg.10.d
	flavor = lia_event_rlg.10.f

	duration = 2
    is_popup = yes
	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/juncha.png"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/africa/city_center"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.10.a
		s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON = {
			create_state = {
				country = c:KOR
				owned_provinces = { 
					"xB05000"
				}
			}
			add_homeland = korean
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_rlg_incheon_a_1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
            s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON = {
                region_state:KOR = {
                    create_building = {
                        building = "building_construction_sector"

	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT

	title = lia_event_rlg.21.t
	desc = lia_event_rlg.21.d
	flavor = lia_event_rlg.21.f

	duration = 2
    is_popup = yes
	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/juncha.png"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/africa/city_center"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.21.a
		s:STATE_LIA_GWANGJU = {
			create_state = {
				country = c:KOR
				owned_provinces = { 
					"x8ACAAA"
				}
			}
			add_homeland = korean
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_rlg_gwangju_a_1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
            s:STATE_LIA_GWANGJU = {
                region_state:KOR = {
                    create_building = {
                        building = "building_construction_sector"
                        level = 1
                    }
                    create_building = {
                        building = "building_trade_center"
                        level = 1
                    }
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_newcity
                        months = 12
                        #is_decaying = yes
                    }
                }
            }
            s:STATE_YANGHO = {
                region_state:KOR = {
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = korean
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:sephardic
                            value = 0.10
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            s:STATE_YANGHO = {
                region_state:KOR = {
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = sephardic
                        }
                        move_pop = s:STATE_LIA_GWANGJU.region_state:KOR
                    }
                }
            }
            s:STATE_LIA_GWANGJU.region_state:KOR = {
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = sephardic
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:korean
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                add_modifier = {
                    name = lia_rlg_modi_gwangju_a_1
                }
            }
            lia_rlg_effect_rural_exodus = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.21.b
		s:STATE_LIA_GWANGJU = {
			create_state = {
				country = c:KOR
				owned_provinces = { 
					"x8ACAAA"
				}
			}
			add_homeland = korean
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_rlg_gwangju_b_1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
            s:STATE_LIA_GWANGJU = {
                region_state:KOR = {
                    create_building = {
                        building = "building_construction_sector"
                        level = 1
                    }

                        level = 1
                    }
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_newcity
                        months = 12

                    }
                }
            }
            s:STATE_YANGHO = {

                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = korean
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:sephardic
                            value = 0.10
                        }

                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_gwangju_b_11

                        limit = {

##30번대는 국고보조금 투입 이벤트 전용 슬롯
lia_event_rlg.30 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT

	title = lia_event_rlg.30.t
	desc = lia_event_rlg.30.desc
	flavor = lia_event_rlg.30.flavor

	duration = 1
    is_popup = yes
	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/juncha.png"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/africa/city_center"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.30.a
        trigger = {
            owns_entire_state_region = STATE_LIA_SEOUL
            s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
                NOT = { has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_support_a }
            }
        }
        
        s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
            add_modifier = {
                name = lia_rlg_modi_support_a
                months = 12
            }
        }
        
        if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
                    has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_seoul_metro_1
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_1
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
                    has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_seoul_metro_2
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_2
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
                    has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_seoul_metro_3
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_3
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
                    has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_seoul_metro_4
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_4
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
                    has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_seoul_metro_5
                    state_population < 2000000
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_5
        }
        else = {
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_6
        }
	}
	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.30.b
        trigger = {
            owns_entire_state_region = STATE_LIA_INCHEON
            s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON.region_state:KOR = {
                NOT = { has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_support_a }
            }
        }
        
        s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON.region_state:KOR = {
            add_modifier = {
                name = lia_rlg_modi_support_a
                months = 12
            }
        }
        
        if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_a_1
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_b_1
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_1
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_a_2
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_b_2
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_2
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_a_3
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_b_3
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_3
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_a_4
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_b_4
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_4
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {

                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_b_5

                    state_population < 2000000

lia_event_rlg.31 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT

	title = lia_event_rlg.31.t
	desc = lia_event_rlg.31.desc
	flavor = lia_event_rlg.31.flavor

	duration = 1
    is_popup = yes
	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/juncha.png"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/africa/city_center"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.31.a
        trigger = {
            owns_entire_state_region = STATE_LIA_SEOUL
        }
        
        hidden_effect = {
            random_scope_state = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_SEOUL
                        state_region = s:STATE_PYONGYANG
                        state_region = s:STATE_SARIWON
                        state_region = s:STATE_BUSAN
                        state_region = s:STATE_YANGHO
                    }
                    state_region = { 
                        is_homeland = cu:korean
                    }
                    state_population >= 2500000
                    OR = {
                        state_unemployment_rate >= 0.025
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 50
                            occupancy >= 0.20
                        }
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 25
                            occupancy >= 0.50
                        }
                    }
                }
                save_scope_as = lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                    add = -100000
                }
            }
            while = {
                limit = {
                    var:lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha >= var:lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                }
                scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor = {
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = korean
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_kor
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = han
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_han
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = manchu
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_man
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = japanese
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_jap
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            OR = {
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_kor
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_man
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap
                            }
                        }
                        move_pop = s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                    multiply = 0.999
                }
            }
            s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_kor
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:korean
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:han
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_man
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:manchu
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:japanese
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
            }
            remove_variable = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
            remove_variable = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
            clear_saved_scope = lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor
        }
        
        if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
                    has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_seoul_metro_1
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_1u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
                    has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_seoul_metro_2
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_2u
        }
        else_if = {

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.31.b
        trigger = {
            owns_entire_state_region = STATE_LIA_INCHEON
        }
        
        hidden_effect = {
            random_scope_state = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_SEOUL
                        state_region = s:STATE_PYONGYANG
                        state_region = s:STATE_SARIWON
                        state_region = s:STATE_BUSAN
                        state_region = s:STATE_YANGHO
                    }
                    state_region = { 
                        is_homeland = cu:korean
                    }
                    state_population >= 2500000
                    OR = {
                        state_unemployment_rate >= 0.025
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 50
                            occupancy >= 0.20
                        }
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 25
                            occupancy >= 0.50
                        }
                    }
                }
                save_scope_as = lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                    add = -100000
                }
            }
            while = {
                limit = {
                    var:lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha >= var:lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                }
                scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor = {
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = korean
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_kor
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = han
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_han
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = manchu
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_man
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = japanese
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_jap
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            OR = {
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_kor
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_man
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap
                            }
                        }
                        move_pop = s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON.region_state:KOR
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                    multiply = 0.999
                }
            }
            s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON.region_state:KOR = {
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_kor
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:korean
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:han
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_man
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:manchu
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:japanese
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
            }
            remove_variable = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
            remove_variable = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
            clear_saved_scope = lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor
        }
        
        if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_a_1
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_b_1
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_1u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_a_2
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_b_2
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_2u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_a_3
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_b_3
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_3u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_a_4
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_b_4
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_4u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON.region_state:KOR = {

                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_a_5
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_b_5

                    state_population < 2000000
                }
            }

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.31.f
        trigger = {
            owns_entire_state_region = STATE_LIA_UIJU
        }
        
        hidden_effect = {
            random_scope_state = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_SEOUL
                        state_region = s:STATE_PYONGYANG
                        state_region = s:STATE_SARIWON
                        state_region = s:STATE_BUSAN
                        state_region = s:STATE_YANGHO
                    }
                    state_region = { 
                        is_homeland = cu:korean
                    }
                    state_population >= 2500000
                    OR = {
                        state_unemployment_rate >= 0.025
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 50
                            occupancy >= 0.20
                        }
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 25
                            occupancy >= 0.50
                        }
                    }
                }
                save_scope_as = lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                    add = -100000
                }
            }
            while = {
                limit = {
                    var:lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha >= var:lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                }
                scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor = {
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = korean
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_kor
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = han
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_han
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = manchu
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_man
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = japanese
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_jap
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            OR = {
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_kor
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_man
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap
                            }
                        }
                        move_pop = s:STATE_LIA_UIJU.region_state:KOR
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                    multiply = 0.999
                }
            }
            s:STATE_LIA_UIJU.region_state:KOR = {
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_kor
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:korean
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:han
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_man
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:manchu
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:japanese
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
            }
            remove_variable = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
            remove_variable = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
            clear_saved_scope = lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor
        }
        
        if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_UIJU.region_state:KOR = {

                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_uiju_b_1

                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_2u

		name = lia_event_rlg.31.j
        trigger = {
            owns_entire_state_region = STATE_LIA_ULSAN
        }
        
        hidden_effect = {
            random_scope_state = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_SEOUL
                        state_region = s:STATE_PYONGYANG
                        state_region = s:STATE_SARIWON
                        state_region = s:STATE_BUSAN
                        state_region = s:STATE_YANGHO
                    }
                    state_region = { 
                        is_homeland = cu:korean
                    }
                    state_population >= 2500000
                    OR = {
                        state_unemployment_rate >= 0.025
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 50
                            occupancy >= 0.20
                        }
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 25
                            occupancy >= 0.50
                        }
                    }
                }
                save_scope_as = lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                    add = -100000
                }
            }
            while = {
                limit = {
                    var:lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha >= var:lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                }
                scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor = {
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = korean
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_kor
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = han
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_han
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = manchu
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_man
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = japanese
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_jap
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            OR = {
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_kor
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_man
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap
                            }
                        }
                        move_pop = s:STATE_LIA_ULSAN.region_state:KOR
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                    multiply = 0.999
                }
            }
            s:STATE_LIA_ULSAN.region_state:KOR = {
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_kor
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:korean
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:han
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_man
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:manchu
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:japanese
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
            }
            remove_variable = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
            remove_variable = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
            clear_saved_scope = lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor
        }
        
        if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_ULSAN.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_ulsan_a_1
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_ulsan_b_1
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_1u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_ULSAN.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_ulsan_a_2
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_ulsan_b_2
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_2u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_ULSAN.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_ulsan_a_3
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_ulsan_b_3
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_3u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_ULSAN.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_ulsan_a_4
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_ulsan_b_4
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_4u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_ULSAN.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_ulsan_a_5
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_ulsan_b_5
                    }
                    state_population < 2000000
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_5u
        }
        else = {
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_6u
        }
	}

            random_scope_state = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_SEOUL
                        state_region = s:STATE_PYONGYANG
                        state_region = s:STATE_SARIWON
                        state_region = s:STATE_BUSAN
                        state_region = s:STATE_YANGHO
                    }
                    state_region = { 
                        is_homeland = cu:korean
                    }
                    state_population >= 2500000
                    OR = {
                        state_unemployment_rate >= 0.025
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 50
                            occupancy >= 0.20
                        }
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 25
                            occupancy >= 0.50
                        }
                    }
                }
                save_scope_as = lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                    add = -100000
                }
            }
            while = {
                limit = {
                    var:lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha >= var:lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                }
                scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor = {
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = korean
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_kor
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = han
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_han
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = manchu
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_man
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = japanese
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_jap
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            OR = {
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_kor
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_man
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap
                            }
                        }
                        move_pop = s:STATE_LIA_JEJU.region_state:KOR
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                    multiply = 0.999
                }
            }
            s:STATE_LIA_JEJU.region_state:KOR = {
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_kor
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:korean
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:han
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_man
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:manchu
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:japanese
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
            }
            remove_variable = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
            remove_variable = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
            clear_saved_scope = lia_rlg_state_movepop_kor
        }
        
        if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_JEJU.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_jeju_a_1
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_jeju_b_1
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_1u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_JEJU.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_jeju_a_2
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_jeju_b_2
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_2u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_JEJU.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_jeju_a_3
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_jeju_b_3
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_3u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_JEJU.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_jeju_a_4
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_jeju_b_4
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_4u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_JEJU.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_jeju_a_5
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_jeju_b_5
                    }
                    state_population < 2000000
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_5u
        }
        else = {
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_6u
        }
	}
    
	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.31.z
        
        trigger_event = {
            id = lia_event_rlg.5
        }
        
        default_option = yes
	}
}

		name = lia_event_rlg.32.e
        trigger = {
            owns_entire_state_region = STATE_LIA_NAMPHO
        }
        
        hidden_effect = {
            random_scope_state = {
                limit = {
                    state_region = { 
                        is_homeland = cu:japanese
                    }
                    state_population >= 2500000
                    OR = {
                        state_unemployment_rate >= 0.025
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 50
                            occupancy >= 0.20
                        }
                        any_scope_building = {

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.32.i
        trigger = {
            owns_entire_state_region = STATE_LIA_BUSAN
        }
        
        hidden_effect = {
            random_scope_state = {
                limit = {
                    state_region = { 
                        is_homeland = cu:japanese
                    }
                    state_population >= 2500000
                    OR = {
                        state_unemployment_rate >= 0.025
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 50
                            occupancy >= 0.20
                        }
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 25
                            occupancy >= 0.50
                        }
                    }
                }
                save_scope_as = lia_rlg_state_movepop_jap
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_jap = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_jap = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                    add = -100000
                }
            }
            while = {
                limit = {
                    var:lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha >= var:lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                }
                scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_jap = {
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = korean
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_kor
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = han
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_han
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = manchu
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_man
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = japanese
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_jap
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            OR = {
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_kor
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_man
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap
                            }
                        }
                        move_pop = s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN.region_state:KOR
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                    multiply = 0.999
                }

            remove_variable = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
            remove_variable = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
            clear_saved_scope = lia_rlg_state_movepop_jap
        }

            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_DAEJEON.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_daejeon_a_1
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_daejeon_b_1
                    }
                }

        else_if = {

		name = lia_event_rlg.32.m
        trigger = {
            owns_entire_state_region = STATE_LIA_GWANGJU
        }
        
        hidden_effect = {
            random_scope_state = {
                limit = {
                    state_region = { 
                        is_homeland = cu:japanese
                    }
                    state_population >= 2500000
                    OR = {

                            level >= 50

                            occupancy >= 0.50

                    }

            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_jap = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_jap = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                    add = -100000
                }
            }

                limit = {
                    var:lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha >= var:lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                }
                scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_jap = {
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = korean
                        }

                            target = cu:wanjang_kor
                            value = 0.001
                        }

                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = han
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {

                            value = 0.001
                        }

                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap
                            }
                        }

                    }

                }

                        target = cu:korean
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:han
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_man
                    }

                        target = cu:manchu
                        value = 1.00
                    }

                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.33.c
        trigger = {
            owns_entire_state_region = STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG

        }
        
        hidden_effect = {
            random_scope_state = {
                limit = {
                    state_region = { 
                        OR = {
                            is_homeland = cu:han
                            is_homeland = cu:manchu
                        }
                    }
                    state_population >= 2500000
                    OR = {
                        state_unemployment_rate >= 0.025
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 50
                            occupancy >= 0.20
                        }
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 25
                            occupancy >= 0.50
                        }
                    }
                }
                save_scope_as = lia_rlg_state_movepop_chi
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_chi = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_chi = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                    add = -100000
                }
            }
            while = {
                limit = {
                    var:lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha >= var:lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                }
                scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_chi = {
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = korean
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_kor
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = han
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_han
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = manchu
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_man
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = japanese
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_jap
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            OR = {
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_kor
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_man
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap
                            }
                        }
                        move_pop = s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG.region_state:KOR
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                    multiply = 0.999
                }
            }
            s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG.region_state:KOR = {
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_kor
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:korean
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:han
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_man
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:manchu
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:japanese
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
            }
            remove_variable = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
            remove_variable = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
            clear_saved_scope = lia_rlg_state_movepop_chi
        }
        
        if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG.region_state:KOR = {
                    has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_pyongyang_metro_1
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_1u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG.region_state:KOR = {
                    has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_pyongyang_metro_2
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_2u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG.region_state:KOR = {
                    has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_pyongyang_metro_3
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_3u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG.region_state:KOR = {
                    has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_pyongyang_metro_4
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_4u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG.region_state:KOR = {
                    has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_pyongyang_metro_5
                    state_population < 2000000
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_5u
        }
        else = {
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_6u
        }
	}

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.33.g
        trigger = {
            owns_entire_state_region = STATE_LIA_NAJIN
        }
        
        hidden_effect = {
            random_scope_state = {
                limit = {
                    state_region = { 
                        OR = {
                            is_homeland = cu:han
                            is_homeland = cu:manchu
                        }
                    }
                    state_population >= 2500000
                    OR = {
                        state_unemployment_rate >= 0.025
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 50
                            occupancy >= 0.20
                        }
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_subsistence_building = yes
                            level >= 25
                            occupancy >= 0.50
                        }
                    }
                }
                save_scope_as = lia_rlg_state_movepop_chi
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_chi = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                value = {
                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_chi = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                    add = -100000
                }
            }
            while = {
                limit = {
                    var:lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha >= var:lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                }
                scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_chi = {
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = korean
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_kor
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = han
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_han
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = manchu
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_man
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = japanese
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_jap
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            OR = {
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_kor
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_man
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap
                            }
                        }
                        move_pop = s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN.region_state:KOR
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
                    multiply = 0.999
                }
            }
            s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN.region_state:KOR = {
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_kor
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:korean
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:han
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_man
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:manchu
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
                every_scope_pop = {
                    limit = {
                        has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap
                    }
                    change_pop_culture = {
                        target = cu:japanese
                        value = 1.00
                    }
                }
            }
            remove_variable = lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha
            remove_variable = lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
            clear_saved_scope = lia_rlg_state_movepop_chi
        }
        
        if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_najin_a_1
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_najin_b_1
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_1u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_najin_a_2
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_najin_b_2
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_2u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_najin_a_3
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_najin_b_3
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_3u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_najin_a_4
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_najin_b_4
                    }
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_4u
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN.region_state:KOR = {
                    OR = {
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_najin_a_5
                        has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_najin_b_5
                    }
                    state_population < 2000000
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_5u
        }
        else = {
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_6u
        }

                    scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_chi = {
                        add = state_population
                    }
                    add = -100000
                }
            }
            while = {
                limit = {
                    var:lia_rlg_city_pop_alpha >= var:lia_rlg_city_pop_beta
                }
                scope:lia_rlg_state_movepop_chi = {
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = korean
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_kor
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_pop_culture = han
                        }
                        change_pop_culture = {
                            target = cu:wanjang_han
                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {

                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }

                            value = 0.001
                        }
                    }
                    every_scope_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            OR = {
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_kor
                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_han
