                                has_pop_culture = wanjang_jap

                        }

                }

	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT

	title = lia_event_rlg.34.t
	desc = lia_event_rlg.34.desc
	flavor = lia_event_rlg.34.flavor

	duration = 1
    is_popup = yes
	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/juncha.png"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/africa/city_center"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.34.a
        trigger = {
            owns_entire_state_region = STATE_LIA_SEOUL
            s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
                NOT = { has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_support_b }
            }
        }
        
        s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
            add_modifier = {
                name = lia_rlg_modi_support_b
                months = 12
            }
        }
        
        if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
                    has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_seoul_metro_1
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_1
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
                    has_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_seoul_metro_2
                }
            }
            add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_2
        }
        else_if = {

####100번대는 서울 개발 관련 이벤트. 100~109는 1단계 저널, 110~119는 2단계 저널, 120~129는 3단계 저널, 이런식으로 149번까지 서울 전용 슬롯
lia_event_rlg.100 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT

	title = lia_event_rlg.100.t
	desc = lia_event_rlg.100.d
	flavor = lia_event_rlg.100.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/juncha.png"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/africa/city_center"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"

	trigger = {
        NOT = { has_variable = lia_var_rlg_seoul_1_a }  #대충 rlg_seoul_1저널의 첫번째 목표를 달성했다는 표시
	}

	immediate = {
        set_variable = lia_var_rlg_seoul_1_a
	}

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.100.a
		default_option = yes

        change_variable = {
            name = lia_var_rlg_seoul_1
            add = 40
        }
	}
}

	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT

	title = lia_event_rlg.114.t
	desc = lia_event_rlg.114.d
	flavor = lia_event_rlg.114.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/rlg/rlg_seoulmainstreet1910.png"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/africa/city_center"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"

	trigger = {
        NOT = { has_technology_researched = electrical_generation }
	}
    
	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.114.a
        
        trigger = {
            can_research = electrical_generation
        }
        
        add_technology_progress = { progress = 12000 technology = electrical_generation }
        add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_5u
        change_variable = {
            name = lia_var_rlg_seoul_2
            add = 10
        }
	}
	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.114.b
        
        trigger = {
            can_research = electrical_generation
        }
        
        add_technology_progress = { progress = 6000 technology = electrical_generation }
        add_treasury = lia_rlg_support_cost_5
        change_variable = {
            name = lia_var_rlg_seoul_2
            add = 10
        }
	}
	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.114.c

        change_variable = {
            name = lia_var_rlg_seoul_2
            add = 10
        }
	}
	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.114.dd
		default_option = yes
        trigger = {
            NOT = { can_research = electrical_generation }
        }
        trigger_event = {
            id = lia_event_rlg.114
            days = 365
        }
	}
}

	type = country_event

	desc = lia_event_rlg.332.d
	flavor = lia_event_rlg.332.f

	trigger = {
        NOT = { has_variable = lia_var_rlg_pyongyang_4_c }
	}

	immediate = {
        set_variable = lia_var_rlg_pyongyang_4_c
	}

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.332.a
		default_option = yes

        change_variable = {
            name = lia_var_rlg_pyongyang_4
            add = 30
        }
		random_list = {
			51 = {
                s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG.region_state:KOR = {
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_pyongyang_win
                    }
                }
                s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_pyongyang_los
                    }
                    add_radicals = {
                        value = 0.10
                    }
                }
                s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL = {
                    add_devastation = 10
                }
			}
			49 = {
                s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_pyongyang_win
                    }
                }
                s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG.region_state:KOR = {
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_pyongyang_los
                    }
                    add_radicals = {
                        value = 0.10
                    }
                }
                s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG = {
                    add_devastation = 10
                }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.332.b

        change_variable = {
            name = lia_var_rlg_pyongyang_4
            add = 30
        }
        random_list = {
			51 = {
                s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_pyongyang_win
                        months = 3
                    }
                }
                s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG.region_state:KOR = {
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_pyongyang_los
                        months = 3
                    }
                    add_radicals = {
                        value = 0.10
                    }
                }
                s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG = {
                    add_devastation = 10
                }
			}
			49 = {
                s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG.region_state:KOR = {
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = lia_rlg_modi_pyongyang_win
                        months = 3
                    }
                }

                    }

                        value = 0.10
                    }
                }

                }

lia_event_rlg.731 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT

	title = lia_event_rlg.731.t
	desc = lia_event_rlg.731.d
	flavor = lia_event_rlg.731.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/juncha.png"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/africa/city_center"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"

	trigger = {
        NOT = { has_variable = lia_var_rlg_najin_4_b }
	}

	immediate = {
        set_variable = lia_var_rlg_najin_4_b
	}

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.731.a
		default_option = yes

        change_variable = {
            name = lia_var_rlg_najin_a_4
            add = 30
        }
        remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_najin_a_fz2
        add_modifier = {
            name = lia_rlg_modi_najin_a_fz3
        }
        add_modifier = {
            name = lia_rlg_modi_najin_a_tsr
        }
        hidden_effect = {
            every_country = {
                limit = {
                    has_state_in_state_region = STATE_MOSCOW
                }
                add_modifier = {
                    name = lia_rlg_modi_najin_a_tsr
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        is_ai = yes
                        NOT = { has_global_variable = trans_siberian_done }
                    }
                    set_global_variable = trans_siberian_done
                    trigger_event = { id = major_railways.1 }
                }
            }
        }
	}
}

lia_event_rlg.782 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT

	title = lia_event_rlg.782.t
	desc = lia_event_rlg.782.d
	flavor = lia_event_rlg.782.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/juncha.png"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/africa/city_center"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"

	trigger = {
        NOT = { has_variable = lia_var_rlg_najin_4_c }
	}

	immediate = {
        set_variable = lia_var_rlg_najin_4_c
	}

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.782.a
		default_option = yes

        change_variable = {
            name = lia_var_rlg_najin_b_4
            add = 30
        }
        add_modifier = {
            name = lia_rlg_modi_najin_b_tsr
        }
        hidden_effect = {
            every_country = {
                limit = {
                    has_state_in_state_region = STATE_MOSCOW
                }
                add_modifier = {
                    name = lia_rlg_modi_najin_b_tsr
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        is_ai = yes
                        NOT = { has_global_variable = trans_siberian_done }
                    }
                    set_global_variable = trans_siberian_done
                    trigger_event = { id = major_railways.1 }
                }
            }
        }
	}
}

	placement = ROOT

	title = lia_event_rlg.1270.t
	desc = lia_event_rlg.1270.d
	flavor = lia_event_rlg.1270.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/juncha.png"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/africa/city_center"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"

	trigger = {
        NOT = { has_variable = lia_var_rlg_daejeon_3_a }
	}

	immediate = {
        set_variable = lia_var_rlg_daejeon_3_a
	}

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.1270.a
		default_option = yes

        change_variable = {
            name = lia_var_rlg_daejeon_b_3
            add = 35
        }
	}
}

        NOT = { has_variable = lia_var_rlg_jeju_3_b }
	}

	immediate = {
        set_variable = lia_var_rlg_jeju_3_b
	}

	option = {
		name = lia_event_rlg.1471.a
		default_option = yes

        change_variable = {
            name = lia_var_rlg_jeju_b_3
            add = 30
        }
        s:STATE_LIA_JEJU.region_state:KOR = {
            add_modifier = {
                name = lia_rlg_modi_jeju_b_civ
            }
        }
	}
}
